    function isPageOf(pageName){

			}

		function layer_show(layer_name,action){
			if(action=="show"){
			   document.getElementById(layer_name).style.visibility="visible";
			}
			else if(action=="hide"){
			   document.getElementById(layer_name).style.visibility="hidden";
			}
		}

				function setStyle(){
					if("$index"=="/index.html"){
							document.getElementById("artisan").src = "http://st.artisancdn.com/template-resources/images/header/logo1.png";
					}else if(isPageOf('index.html')){
							document.getElementById("&lt;a href='/' class='hh1'&gt;Home&lt;/a&gt;").innerHTML = "";

						document.getElementById("support").className = "hh2";

				}
								getUserInfo(0);
   </script>

   function setIframeSrc() {
		var s = "http://player.vimeo.com/video/78279483?title=0&amp;byline=0&amp;portrait=0";
		var playerFrame = document.getElementById('playerFrame');
		if ( - 1 == navigator.userAgent.indexOf("MSIE")) {
			playerFrame.src = s;
		} else {
			playerFrame.location = s;
		}
	}

	function   ostPrice(oprice,sprice,tprice){
		oprice = changeTwoDecimal(oprice);
		sprice = changeTwoDecimal(sprice);
		tprice = changeTwoDecimal(tprice);
		var str = '';
		str = str + '&lt;div style="width:750px;height:60px;float:left;line-height:60px;text-align:center;"&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="strikeout" id="oprice"&gt;&nbsp;$'+oprice+'&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:15px;"&gt;&nbsp;(Regular Price)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:40px;font-weight:bold;" id="lprice"&gt;$'+sprice+'&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;a class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:15px;" href="/special-offer.html" target="_self"&gt;&nbsp;&nbsp;(On Sale &gt;)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;/a&gt;';
		str = str +		'&lt;span class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:40px;font-weight:bold;" id="lprice"&gt;$'+5+'&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;a class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:15px;" href="/low-cost.html" target="_self"&gt;&nbsp;&nbsp;(New User Trial &gt;)&lt;/a&gt;';
		str = str + '&lt;/div&gt;';
		return str;
	}
	function   osPrice(oprice,sprice){
		var str = '';
		oprice = changeTwoDecimal(oprice);
		sprice = changeTwoDecimal(sprice);
		str = str + '&lt;div style="width:750px;height:60px;float:left;line-height:60px;text-align:center;"&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="strikeout" id="oprice" style="font-size:40px;font-weight:bold;"&gt;&nbsp;$'+oprice+'&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:15px;"&gt;&nbsp;(Regular Price)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="fonts-z109" style="font-weight:bold;font-size:40px;" id="lprice"&gt;$'+sprice+'&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;a class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:15px;" href="/special-offer.html" target="_self"&gt;&nbsp;&nbsp;(New User Trial &gt;)&lt;/a&gt;';
		str = str + '&lt;/div&gt;';
		return str;
	}
	function   oPrice(oprice){
		oprice = changeTwoDecimal(oprice);
		var str = '';
		str = str + '&lt;div style="width:750px;height:60px;float:left;line-height:60px;text-align:center;"&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="fonts-z109" id="oprice" style="font-size:40px;font-weight:bold;"&gt;&nbsp;$'+oprice+'&nbsp;&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + 	'&lt;span class="fonts-z109" style="font-size:15px;"  target="_self"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;';
		str = str + '&lt;/div&gt;';
		return str;
	}
	function changeTwoDecimal(x){
		var s_x = x.toString();
		var pos_decimal = s_x.indexOf('.');
		if (pos_decimal &gt; 0){
			s_x = x.toFixed(2);
		}
		return s_x;
	}

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function redirect(url){
					window.location.href=url;
					if(isPageOf('support.html')){
						window.location.reload();
					}
				}
				if(isPageOf('/flush-mount.html')){
					document.getElementById("foot-flush-mount").className = "bar2";
				}else if(isPageOf('/terms.html')){
					document.getElementById("foottermsofuse").className = "bar2";
				}else if(isPageOf('/privacy.html')){
					document.getElementById("footprivacypolicy").className = "bar2";
				}else if(isPageOf('/membership.html')){
					document.getElementById("footmembership").className = "bar2";
				}else if(isPageOf('/pro-plan.html')){
					document.getElementById("footproplan").className = "bar2";
